 kshetrafal ke lihaaj se yah uttar pradesh kaa sabase chota jila he or gyanpur shahar jila mukhyalay he
 The district of Bhadohi is situated on the plains of the river Ganges, forming the southwestern boundary of the district
 ganga ke alaava varun or morva yahaan kii pramukh nadiyaan hai

 jaaniye jain dharm kii is pratha kii 10 khaas baaten
 1
 jain dharmamen do panth hai, shwetambar or digambar
 Santhara is prevalent in the Svetambaras

 2

 The person taking the santhara gradually reduces his food
 3
 According to Jain texts, in Santhara the person is given food according to the rule
 ann band karne se matlab usee sthiti se hota he, jab ann kaa pachan sambhav na rah jaae
 4
 bhagwaan mahavir ke upadeshaanusaar janm kii tarah mrityu ko bhi utsav kaa rup diya ja saktaa he
 The person who takes Santhara will also be able to succeed on his last journey, thinking that Santhara is taken
 5
 In Jainism, Santhara is not counted in any fast
 6

 is vrath ko naukaarthi kaha jaataa he
 7
 santhara main upwas pani ke saath or bina pani pie, donon tareekon se ho saktaa he
 8
 santhara lene se pehle parivaar or guru kii ajna leni jaruri hoti he
 9
 yah swechha se deh tyaagane kii parampara he
 In Jainism, it is considered the ultimate practice of life
 10
 According to Jainism, as long as any real treatment is possible, then that non-violent treatment should be done
